Note
7 - Line of Credit

Effective
January 3
 2014
 the Company entered into a Sale and Security Agreement (the &ldquo;Sale and Security Agreement&rdquo;) with Faunus
Group International
 Inc. (&ldquo;FGI&rdquo;) to provide for a $1.5 million secured demand credit facility backed by its receivables
and inventory (the &ldquo;FGI Facility&rdquo;). The Sale and Security Agreement has an initial three year term (the &ldquo;Original
Term&rdquo;) and shall be extended automatically for an additional one year for each succeeding term unless written notice of
termination is given by either party at least sixty days prior to the end of the Original Term or any extension thereof. The Company
and certain of its affiliates also entered into guarantees to guarantee the performance of the obligations under the Sale and
Security Agreement (the &ldquo;Guaranty Agreements&rdquo;). The Company also granted FGI a security interest in and lien upon
all of the Company&rsquo;s right
 title and interest in and to all of its assets (as defined in the Sale and Security Agreement).

Pursuant
to the FGI Facility
 FGI can elect to purchase eligible accounts receivables (&ldquo;Purchased Accounts&rdquo;) up to 70% of the
value of such receivables (retaining a 30% reserve). At FGI&rsquo;s election
 FGI may advance the Company up to 70% of the value
of any Purchased Accounts
 subject to the FGI Facility. Reserves retained by FGI on any Purchased Accounts are expected to be
refunded to the Company net of interest and fees on advances once the receivables are collected from customers. The interest rate
on advances or borrowings under the FGI Facility will be the greater of (i) 6.75% per annum and (ii) 2.50% above the prime rate.
Any advances or borrowings under the FGI Facility are due on demand.

The
Company also agreed to pay to FGI monthly collateral management fees of 0.42% of the average monthly balance of Purchased Accounts.
The minimum monthly net funds employed during each contract year hereof shall be $500
000. Additionally
 the Company paid FGI
a one-time facility fee equal to 1% of the FGI Facility upon entry into the Sale and Security Agreement.

During
the year ended January 31
 2015
 the Company terminated its agreement with FGI and paid off all obligations due at the payoff
date. Upon termination
 additional fees and accrued interest of approximately $48
600 were paid and included in the interest expense.

noted in Note 8

 2014

000 shares of restricted common stock
were issued to Manatuck. Based on management&rsquo;s review
 the accounting for debt modification applied. The Company valued
the 30

600 to debt discount on the consolidated balance sheet.

Upon
issuance of the debenture and subsequent extension
 a debt discount of $498
350 was recorded for the fees incurred by the buyer
as well as the value of the common shares granted to Manatuck. The debt discount will be amortized over the earlier of (i) the
term of the debt or (ii) conversion of the debt
 using the straight-line method which approximates the effective interest method.
The amortization of debt discount is included as a component of interest expense in the consolidated statements of operations.
There was unamortized debt discount of $0 and $412
553 as of January 31
 2016 and 2015
 respectively.

On
October 29
 2015
 the note was further amended to extend the maturity date to December 19

of the extension

000 shares issued to Manatuck for a share price of $0.65
a value of $149
500 and incurred an amendment fee of $170
500
 both of which were added to the outstanding principal of the debt.
In addition
 the extension reduced accrued interest by $220
000 and increased the outstanding principal of the debt by $220
000.
The outstanding principal at January 31
 2016 was $2
540
000. Based on management&rsquo;s review
 the accounting for debt extinguishment
applied. In accordance with the accounting for debt extinguishment
 the Company wrote-off the existing debt of $2
000
000
 wrote-off
the unamortized debt discount of $190
483 and wrote-off the remaining debt issuance costs relating to this note of $19
106. The
loss on debt extinguishment of $380
089 on the statement of operations is comprised of the write-off of the remaining debt discount
of $190
483

106
 and the amendment fee of $170
500.

conversion to convertible preferred stock is available upon completion of a qualified offering (as defined in the Manatuck Purchase

 the Company shall issue Manatuck
shares of common stock as defined in the Manatuck Purchase Agreement.

 2015

 as

 combinations

 the Company concluded that equity treatment
was warranted since the feature was clearly and closely related to the host contract. The holders of the Series Preferred A will

 (b) a liquidation preference equal to $100.00 per Series

 (c) the option to convert the Series A Preferred shares to a number of shares of common
stock calculated by dividing the Stated Value by $0.675 and (d) warrants to purchase a number of common shares calculated by
dividing the Stated Value by $0.675 exercisable for a period of five years at a price of $1.00 per share. There is also an automatic
conversion based on the occurrence of certain events detailed in the Certificate of Designation. As of January 31

992.

Note
12 - Commitments and Contingencies

Litigations
Claims and Assessments

From
time to time
 the Company may become involved in various lawsuits and legal proceedings
 which arise in the ordinary course of
business. Litigation is subject to inherent uncertainties
 and an adverse result in these or other matters may arise from time
to time that may harm its business. The Company is currently not aware of any such legal proceedings or claims that they believe
will have
 individually or in the aggregate
 a material adverse effect on its business
 financial condition or operating results.

Licensing
and Royalty Agreements

On
March 1
 2010
 the Company was assigned a Development and License agreement (the &ldquo;Agreement&rdquo;). Under the terms of
the Agreement the Licensor shall develop for the Company a line of beef meatballs with sauce
 turkey meatballs with sauce and
other similar meats and sauces for commercial manufacture
 distribution and sale (each a &ldquo;Licensor Product&rdquo; and collectively
the &ldquo;Licensor Products&rdquo;). Licensor shall work with Licensee to develop Licensor Products that are acceptable to Licensee.
Upon acceptance of a Licensor Product by Licensee
 Licensor&rsquo;s trade secret recipes
 formulas methods and ingredients for
the preparation and production of such Licensor Products (the &ldquo;Recipes&rdquo;) shall be subject to this Development and
License Agreement.

The
term of the Agreement (the &ldquo;Term&rdquo;) shall consist of the Exclusive Term and the Non-Exclusive Term. The 12-month period
beginning on each January 1 and ending on each December 31 is referred to herein as an &ldquo;Agreement Year&rdquo;.

The
Exclusive Term began on January 1
 2009 (the &ldquo;Effective Date&rdquo;) and ends on the 50th anniversary of the Effective Date
unless terminated or extended as provided herein. Licensor
 at its option
 may terminate the Exclusive Term by notice in writing
to Licensee
 delivered between the 60th and the 90th day following the end of any Agreement Year if
 on or before the 60th day
following the end of such Agreement Year
 Licensee has not paid Licensor Royalties with respect to such Agreement Year at least
equal to the minimum royalty (the &ldquo;Minimum Royalty&rdquo;) for such Agreement Year. Subject to the foregoing sentence
 and
provided Licensee has not breached this Agreement and failed to cure such breach in accordance herewith
 Licensee may extend the
Exclusive Term for an additional twenty five (25) years
 by notice in writing to Licensor
 delivered on or before the 50th anniversary
of the Effective Date.

The
Non-Exclusive Term begins upon expiration of the Exclusive Term and continues indefinitely thereafter
 until terminated by Licensor
due to a material breach hereof by Licensee that remains uncured after notice and opportunity to cure in accordance herewith
or until terminated by Licensee.


    
    


MamaMancini&rsquo;s
Holdings
 Inc.
Notes
to Consolidated Financial Statements
January
31
 2016

Either
party may terminate this Agreement in the event that the other party materially breaches its obligations and fails to cure such
material breach within sixty (60) days following written notice from the non-breaching party specifying the nature of the breach.
The following termination rights are in addition to the termination rights provided elsewhere in the agreement



    
    
Termination by Licensee
    - Licensee shall have the right to terminate this Agreement at any time on sixty (60) days written notice to Licensor. In
    such event
 all moneys paid to Licensor shall be deemed non-refundable.


Under
the terms of the Agreement the Company is required to pay quarterly royalty fees as follows:

During
the Exclusive Term and the Non-Exclusive Term the Company will pay a royalty equal to the royalty rate (the &ldquo;Royalty Rate&rdquo;)
multiplied by Company&rsquo;s &ldquo;Net Sales&rdquo;. As used herein
 &ldquo;Net Sales&rdquo; means gross invoiced sales of Products
directly or indirectly to unrelated third parties
 less (a) discounts (including cash discounts)
 and retroactive price reductions
or allowances actually allowed or granted from the billed amount (collectively &ldquo;Discounts&rdquo;); (b) credits
 rebates
and allowances actually granted upon claims
 rejections or returns
 including recalls (voluntary or otherwise) (collectively
&ldquo;Credits&rdquo;); (c) freight
 postage
 shipping and insurance charges; (d) taxes
 duties or other governmental charges
levied on or measured by the billing amount
 when included in billing
 as adjusted for rebates and refunds; and (e) provisions
for uncollectible accounts determined in accordance with reasonable accounting methods
 consistently applied.

The
Royalty Rate shall be: 6% of net sales up to $500
000 of net sales for each Agreement year; 4% of Net Sales from $500
000 up to
$2
500
000 of Net Sales for each Agreement year; 2% of Net Sales from $2
500
000 up to $20
000
000 of Net Sales for each Agreement
year; and 1% of Net Sales in excess of $20
000
000 of Net Sales for each Agreement year.

order to continue the Exclusive term
 the Company shall pay a minimum royalty with respect to the preceding Agreement year as

The
Company has U.S. federal net operating loss carryovers (NOLs) of approximately $12.9M and $8.8M at January 31
 2016 and 2015
respectively
 available to offset taxable income through 2034. If not used
 these NOLs may be subject to limitation under Internal
Revenue Code Section 382 should there be a greater than 50% ownership change as determined under the regulations. The Company
plans on undertaking a detailed analysis of any historical and/or current Section 382 ownership changes that may limit the utilization
of the net operating loss carryovers. The Company also has New Jersey State Net Operating Loss carry overs of $12.9M and $8.8M
at January 31
 2016 and 2015
 respectively
 available to offset future taxable income through 2034.

In
assessing the realization of deferred tax assets
 management considers whether it is more likely than not that some portion or
all of the deferred tax assets will not be realized. The ultimate realization of deferred tax assets is dependent upon future
generation for taxable income during the periods in which temporary differences representing net future deductible amounts become
deductible. Management considers the scheduled reversal of deferred tax liabilities
 projected future taxable income and tax planning
strategies in making this assessment. After consideration of all the information available
 Management believes that significant
uncertainty exists with respect to future realization of the deferred tax assets and has therefore established a full valuation
allowance. For the year ended January 31
 2016 and 2015
 the change in the valuation allowance was $1
405
640and $1
745
469.


    
    


MamaMancini&rsquo;s
Holdings
 Inc.
Notes
to Consolidated Financial Statements

The
Company evaluated the provisions of ASC 740 related to the accounting for uncertainty in income taxes recognized in an enterprise&rsquo;s
financial statements. ASC 740 prescribes a comprehensive model for how a company should recognize
 present
 and disclose uncertain
positions that the Company has taken or expects to take in its tax return. For those benefits to be recognized
 a tax position
must be more-likely-than-not to be sustained upon examination by taxing authorities. Differences between tax positions taken or
expected to be taken in a tax return and the net benefit recognized and measured pursuant to the interpretation are referred to
as &ldquo;unrecognized benefits.&rdquo; A liability is recognized (or amount of net operating loss carry forward or amount of
tax refundable is reduced) for unrecognized tax benefit because it represents an enterprise&rsquo;s potential future obligation
to the taxing authority for a tax position that was not recognized as a result of applying the provisions of ASC 740.

If
applicable
 interest costs related to the unrecognized tax benefits are required to be calculated and would be classified as &ldquo;Other
expenses &ndash; Interest&rdquo; in the statement of operations. Penalties would be recognized as a component of &ldquo;General
and administrative.&rdquo;

No
interest or penalties on unpaid tax were recorded during the year ended January 31
 2016 and 2015
 respectively. As of January
31
 2016 and 2015
 no liability for unrecognized tax benefits was required to be reported. The Company does not expect any significant
changes in its unrecognized tax benefits in the next year.

The
Company&rsquo;s deferred tax assets (liabilities) consisted of the effects of temporary differences attributable to the following:

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Note 12 - Commitments and Contingencies&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Litigations, Claims and Assessments&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;From time to time, the Company may become&#13;involved in various lawsuits and legal proceedings, which arise in the ordinary course of business. Litigation is subject to inherent&#13;uncertainties, and an adverse result in these or other matters may arise from time to time that may harm its business. The Company&#13;is currently not aware of any such legal proceedings or claims that they believe will have, individually or in the aggregate, a&#13;material adverse effect on its business, financial condition or operating results.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Licensing and Royalty Agreements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On March 1, 2010, the Company was assigned&#13;a Development and License agreement (the &amp;#147;Agreement&amp;#148;). Under the terms of the Agreement the Licensor shall develop&#13;for the Company a line of beef meatballs with sauce, turkey meatballs with sauce and other similar meats and sauces for commercial&#13;manufacture, distribution and sale (each a &amp;#147;Licensor Product&amp;#148; and collectively the &amp;#147;Licensor Products&amp;#148;).&#13;Licensor shall work with Licensee to develop Licensor Products that are acceptable to Licensee. Upon acceptance of a Licensor Product&#13;by Licensee, Licensor&amp;#146;s trade secret recipes, formulas methods and ingredients for the preparation and production of such&#13;Licensor Products (the &amp;#147;Recipes&amp;#148;) shall be subject to this Development and License Agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The term of the Agreement (the &amp;#147;Term&amp;#148;)&#13;shall consist of the Exclusive Term and the Non-Exclusive Term. The 12-month period beginning on each January 1 and ending on each&#13;December 31 is referred to herein as an &amp;#147;Agreement Year&amp;#148;.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Exclusive Term began on January&#13;1, 2009 (the &amp;#147;Effective Date&amp;#148;) and ends on the 50th anniversary of the Effective Date, unless terminated or extended&#13;as provided herein. Licensor, at its option, may terminate the Exclusive Term by notice in writing to Licensee, delivered between&#13;the 60th and the 90th day following the end of any Agreement Year if, on or before the 60th day following the end of such Agreement&#13;Year, Licensee has not paid Licensor Royalties with respect to such Agreement Year at least equal to the minimum royalty (the &amp;#147;Minimum&#13;Royalty&amp;#148;) for such Agreement Year. Subject to the foregoing sentence, and provided Licensee has not breached this Agreement&#13;and failed to cure such breach in accordance herewith, Licensee may extend the Exclusive Term for an additional twenty five (25)&#13;years, by notice in writing to Licensor, delivered on or before the 50th anniversary of the Effective Date.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Non-Exclusive Term begins upon expiration&#13;of the Exclusive Term and continues indefinitely thereafter, until terminated by Licensor due to a material breach hereof by Licensee&#13;that remains uncured after notice and opportunity to cure in accordance herewith, or until terminated by Licensee.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Either party may terminate this Agreement&#13;in the event that the other party materially breaches its obligations and fails to cure such material breach within sixty (60)&#13;days following written notice from the non-breaching party specifying the nature of the breach. The following termination rights&#13;are in addition to the termination rights provided elsewhere in the agreement&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px; font: 10pt/115% Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px; font: 10pt/115% Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=font: 10pt/115% Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;Termination by Licensee - Licensee shall have the right to terminate this Agreement at any time on sixty (60) days written notice to Licensor. In such event, all moneys paid to Licensor shall be deemed non-refundable.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Under the terms of the Agreement the&#13;Company is required to pay quarterly royalty fees as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;During the Exclusive Term and the Non-Exclusive&#13;Term the Company will pay a royalty equal to the royalty rate (the &amp;#147;Royalty Rate&amp;#148;), multiplied by Company&amp;#146;s &amp;#147;Net&#13;Sales&amp;#148;. As used herein, &amp;#147;Net Sales&amp;#148; means gross invoiced sales of Products, directly or indirectly to unrelated&#13;third parties, less (a) discounts (including cash discounts), and retroactive price reductions or allowances actually allowed or&#13;granted from the billed amount (collectively &amp;#147;Discounts&amp;#148;); (b) credits, rebates, and allowances actually granted upon&#13;claims, rejections or returns, including recalls (voluntary or otherwise) (collectively, &amp;#147;Credits&amp;#148;); (c) freight, postage,&#13;shipping and insurance charges; (d) taxes, duties or other governmental charges levied on or measured by the billing amount, when&#13;included in billing, as adjusted for rebates and refunds; and (e) provisions for uncollectible accounts determined in accordance&#13;with reasonable accounting methods, consistently applied.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Royalty Rate shall be: 6% of net&#13;sales up to $500,000 of net sales for each Agreement year; 4% of Net Sales from $500,000 up to $2,500,000 of Net Sales for each&#13;Agreement year; 2% of Net Sales from $2,500,000 up to $20,000,000 of Net Sales for each Agreement year; and 1% of Net Sales in&#13;excess of $20,000,000 of Net Sales for each Agreement year.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In order to continue the Exclusive term,&#13;the Company shall pay a minimum royalty with respect to the preceding Agreement year as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

   &lt;td style=text-align: right; line-height: 115%&gt;125,000&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company incurred $271,880 and $&#13;284,861 of royalty expenses for the year ended January 31, 2016 and 2015. Royalty expenses are included in general and administrative&#13;expenses on the consolidated statement of operations.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Agreements with Placement Agents&#13;and Finders&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in&gt;(A) April 1, 2015&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company entered into a fourth Financial&#13;Advisory and Investment Banking Agreement with Spartan Capital Securities, LLC (&amp;#147;Spartan&amp;#148;) effective April 1, 2015&#13;(the &amp;#147;Spartan Advisory Agreement&amp;#148;). Pursuant to the Spartan Advisory Agreement, the Company shall pay to Spartan a&#13;non-refundable monthly fee of $10,000 through October 1, 2015. The monthly fee shall survive any termination of the Agreement.&#13;Additionally, (i) if at least $4,000,000 is raised in the Financing, the Company shall pay to Spartan a non-refundable fee of $5,000&#13;per month from November 1, 2015 through October 2017; and (ii) if at least $5,000,000 is raised in the Financing, the Company shall&#13;pay to Spartan a non-refundable fee of $5,000 per month from November 1, 2017 through October 2019. If $10,000,000 or more is raised&#13;in the Financing, the Company shall issue to Spartan shares of its common stock having an aggregate value of $5,000 (as determined&#13;by reference to the average volume weighted average trading price for the last five trading days of the immediately preceding month)&#13;on the first day of each month during the period from November 1, 2015 through October 1, 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company upon closing of the Financing&#13;shall pay consideration to Spartan, in cash, a fee in an amount equal to 10% of the aggregate gross proceeds raised in the Financing&#13;and 3% of the aggregate gross proceeds raised in the Financing for expenses incurred by Spartan. The Company shall grant and deliver&#13;to Spartan at the closing of the Financing, for nominal consideration, five year warrants to purchase a number of shares of the&#13;Company&amp;#146;s common stock equal to 10% of the number of shares of common stock (and/or shares of common stock issuable upon&#13;exercise of securities or upon conversion or exchange of convertible or exchangeable securities) sold at such closing. The warrants&#13;shall be exercisable at any time during the five year period commencing on the closing to which they relate at an exercise price&#13;equal to the purchase price per share of common stock paid by investors in the Financing or, in the case of exercisable, convertible,&#13;or exchangeable securities, the exercise, conversion or exchange price thereof. If the Financing is consummated by means of more&#13;than one closing, Spartan shall be entitled to the fees provided herein with respect to each such closing.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;During the year ended January 31, 2016,&#13;the Company paid to Spartan a one-time engagement fee of $10,000. In connection with the Initial Closing, the Company agreed to&#13;pay an aggregate cash fee and non-accountable allowance of $157,300. The Company also granted warrants to purchase 179,259 shares&#13;of common stock at $0.675 per share. The warrants have a grant date fair value of $84,547 which is treated as a direct cost of&#13;the Financing and has been recorded as a reduction in additional paid in capital.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In January 2015, the Company began a&#13;lease agreement for office space in East Rutherford, NJ. The lease is for a 51 month term expiring on March 31, 2019 with annual&#13;payments of $18,848.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In order to continue the Exclusive term,&#13;the Company shall pay a minimum royalty with respect to the preceding Agreement year as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Note 11 - Stockholders&amp;#146;&#13;Equity (Deficit)&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;(A) Series A Convertible Preferred&#13;Stock Transactions&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On May 28, 2015, the Company amended&#13;its articles of incorporation to establish the designation, powers, rights, privileges, preferences and restrictions of the Series&#13;A Convertible Preferred Stock (&amp;#147;Series A Preferred&amp;#148;). The Company authorized 120,000 shares of Series A Preferred with&#13;each share of our Series A Preferred having a par value of $0.00001 and stated value equal to $100 (&amp;#147;Stated Value&amp;#148;),&#13;as adjusted for stock dividends, combinations, splits and certain other events. The Company analyzed the conversion feature for&#13;potential derivative classification. Despite the ratchet features included in the conversion option, the Company concluded that&#13;equity treatment was warranted since the feature was clearly and closely related to the host contract. The holders of the Series&#13;Preferred A will be entitled to (a) dividends at a rate of 8% per annum, (b) a liquidation preference equal to $100.00 per Series&#13;A Preferred share, (c) the option to convert the Series A Preferred shares to a number of shares of common stock calculated by&#13;dividing the Stated Value by $0.675 and (d) warrants to purchase a number of common shares calculated by dividing the Stated Value&#13;by $0.675 exercisable for a period of five years at a price of $1.00 per share. There is also an automatic conversion based on&#13;the occurrence of certain events detailed in the Certificate of Designation. As of January 31, 2016, dividends in arrears totaled&#13;$66,992.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;During May 2015, six directors of the&#13;Company entered into convertible note agreements with a maturity date of July 22, 2016 for total proceeds to the Company of $650,000.&#13;In June 2015, the notes were converted into Series A Preferred. Additional proceeds of $560,000 were received pursuant to closings&#13;that occurred in June, August and September. In connection with the closings, the Company also granted warrants to purchase 1,481,481&#13;and 179,259 shares of common stock at $0.675 per share to shareholders and the placement agent, respectively. The warrants granted&#13;to the placement agent have a grant date fair value of $84,547 which is treated as a direct cost of the Financing and has been&#13;recorded as a reduction in additional paid in capital.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;During November 2015, the Company completed&#13;the final closing of a private placement with 11 accredited investors and issued an aggregate of 10,200 shares of Series A Preferred&#13;and warrants to purchase 1,511,112 shares of common stock for aggregate gross proceeds to the Company of $1,020,000. Stock issuance&#13;costs of $132,600 were paid to placement agents yielding net proceeds of $887,400. Of these issuance costs, approximately $86,000&#13;were pursuant to the promissory note agreement as discussed in Note 6.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;As discussed in Note 6, during January&#13;2016, the Company settled an outstanding payable with one of its vendors by issuing a promissory note in the principal amount of&#13;$116,003 and 1,100 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s Series A Preferred and warrants to purchase 162,963 shares of common stock.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On December 19, 2014, the Company issued&#13;a convertible redeemable debenture (the &amp;#147;Manatuck Debenture&amp;#148; as discussed in Note 8). Upon issuance of the Manatuck&#13;Debenture, the Company granted Manatuck 200,000 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s restricted common stock. In April 2015 the maturity&#13;date of the note was extended until May 2016. Upon execution of the extension, the Company granted Manatuck 30,000 shares of the&#13;Company&amp;#146;s restricted common stock with a grant date fair value of $39,600.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;During the year ended January 31, 2016,&#13;the Company issued 8,540 shares of its common stock for a cashless conversion of 22,666 warrants.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;During the year ended January 31, 2016,&#13;the Company issued 421,600 shares of its common stock to employees for services rendered a value of $242,487.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The following is a summary of the Company&amp;#146;s&#13;option activity:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Note 2 - Summary of Significant&#13;Accounting Policies&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of Estimates&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The preparation of consolidated financial&#13;statements in conformity with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles requires management to make estimates and assumptions&#13;that affect the amounts reported in the consolidated financial statements and accompanying notes. Such estimates and assumptions&#13;impact, among others, the following: allowance for doubtful accounts, inventory obsolescence and the fair value of share-based&#13;payments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Making estimates requires management&#13;to exercise significant judgment. It is at least reasonably possible that the estimate of the effect of a condition, situation&#13;or set of circumstances that existed at the date of the consolidated financial statements, which management considered in formulating&#13;its estimate could change in the near term due to one or more future confirming events. Accordingly, the actual results could differ&#13;significantly from our estimates.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Risks and Uncertainties&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company operates in an industry&#13;that is subject to intense competition and change in consumer demand. The Company&amp;#146;s operations are subject to significant&#13;risk and uncertainties including financial and operational risks including the potential risk of business failure.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company has experienced, and in&#13;the future expects to continue to experience, variability in sales and earnings. The factors expected to contribute to this variability&#13;include, among others, (i) the cyclical nature of the grocery industry, (ii) general economic conditions in the various local markets&#13;in which the Company competes, including the general downturn in the economy, and (iii) the volatility of prices pertaining to&#13;food and beverages in connection with the Company&amp;#146;s distribution of the product. These factors, among others, make it difficult&#13;to project the Company&amp;#146;s operating results on a consistent basis.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company considers all highly liquid&#13;instruments purchased with a maturity of three months or less to be cash equivalents. The Company held no cash equivalents at January&#13;31, 2016 or January 31, 2015.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company minimizes its credit risk&#13;associated with cash by periodically evaluating the credit quality of its primary financial institution. The balance at times may&#13;exceed federally insured limits.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Accounts Receivable and Allowance&#13;for Doubtful Accounts&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Accounts receivable are stated at the&#13;amount management expects to collect from outstanding balances. The Company generally does not require collateral to support customer&#13;receivables. The Company provides an allowance for doubtful accounts based upon a review of the outstanding accounts receivable,&#13;historical collection information and existing economic conditions. The Company determines if receivables are past due based on&#13;days outstanding, and amounts are written off when determined to be uncollectible by management. The maximum accounting loss from&#13;the credit risk associated with accounts receivable is the amount of the receivable recorded, which is the face amount of the receivable&#13;net of the allowance for doubtful accounts. As of January 31, 2016 and 2015, the Company had reserves of $2,000.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Inventories&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Inventories are stated at average cost&#13;using the first-in, first-out (FIFO) valuation method. Inventory was comprised of the following at January 31, 2016 and January&#13;31, 2015:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Property and Equipment&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Property and equipment are recorded&#13;at cost. Depreciation expense is computed using straight-line methods over the estimated useful lives.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in&gt;Asset lives for&#13;financial statement reporting of depreciation are:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 61%; line-height: 115%&gt;Machinery and equipment&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%; text-align: justify; line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 38%; text-align: justify; line-height: 115%&gt;2-7 years&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;Furniture and fixtures&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; line-height: 115%&gt;3-5 years&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;Leasehold improvements&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify; line-height: 115%&gt;3-10 years&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair Value of Financial Instruments&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;For purpose of this disclosure, the&#13;fair value of a financial instrument is the amount at which the instrument could be exchanged in a current transaction between&#13;willing parties, other than in a forced sale or liquidation. The carrying amount of the Company&amp;#146;s short term financial instruments&#13;approximates fair value due to the relatively short period to maturity for these instruments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock Issuance Costs&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Stock issuance costs are capitalized&#13;as incurred. Upon the completion of the offering, the stock issuance costs are reclassified to equity and netted against proceeds.&#13;In the event the costs are in excess of the proceeds, the costs are recorded to expense. In the case of an aborted offering, all&#13;costs are expensed. Offering costs recorded to equity for the year ended January 31, 2016 and 2015 were $678,099 and $346,192,&#13;respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Research and Development&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Research and development is expensed&#13;as incurred. Research and development expenses for the year ended January 31, 2016 and 2015 were $107,632 and $100,864, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Shipping and Handling Costs&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company classifies freight billed&#13;to customers as sales revenue and the related freight costs as cost of sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenue Recognition&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company records revenue for products&#13;when all of the following have occurred: (1) persuasive evidence of an arrangement exists, (2) the product is delivered, (3) the&#13;sales price to the customer is fixed or determinable, and (4) collectability of the related customer receivable is reasonably assured.&#13;There is no stated right of return for products.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company meets these criteria upon&#13;shipment.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Expenses such as slotting fees, sales&#13;discounts, and allowances are accounted for as a direct reduction of revenues as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cost of Sales&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Cost of sales represents costs directly&#13;related to the production and manufacturing of the Company&amp;#146;s products. Costs include product development, freight, packaging,&#13;and print production costs.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Advertising&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Costs incurred for producing and communicating&#13;advertising for the Company are charged to operations as incurred. Producing and communicating advertising expenses for the year&#13;ended January 31, 2016 and 2015 were $2,096,026 and $2,774,356, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock-Based Compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company accounts for stock-based&#13;compensation in accordance with ASC Topic 718, &amp;#147;Compensation &amp;#150; Stock Compensation&amp;#148; (&amp;#147;ASC 718&amp;#148;) which&#13;establishes financial accounting and reporting standards for stock-based employee compensation. It defines a fair value based method&#13;of accounting for an employee stock option or similar equity instrument. The Company accounts for compensation cost for stock option&#13;plans in accordance with ASC 718. The Company accounts for share-based payments to non-employees in accordance with ASC 505-50&#13;&amp;#147;Equity Based Payments to Non-Employees&amp;#148;.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company recognizes all forms of&#13;share-based payments, including stock option grants, warrants and restricted stock grants, at their fair value on the grant date,&#13;which are based on the estimated number of awards that are ultimately expected to vest.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Share-based payments, excluding restricted&#13;stock, are valued using a Black-Scholes option pricing model. Grants of share-based payment awards issued to non-employees for&#13;services rendered have been recorded at the fair value of the share-based payment, which is the more readily determinable value.&#13;The grants are amortized on a straight-line basis over the requisite service periods, which is generally the vesting period. If&#13;an award is granted, but vesting does not occur, any previously recognized compensation cost is reversed in the period related&#13;to the termination of service. Stock-based compensation expenses are included in cost of goods sold or selling, general and administrative&#13;expenses, depending on the nature of the services provided, in the consolidated statement of operations. Share-based payments issued&#13;to placement agents are classified as a direct cost of a stock offering and are recorded as a reduction in additional paid in capital.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;For the year ended January 31, 2016&#13;and 2015, share-based compensation amounted to $487,316 and $438,343, respectively. Of the $487,316, and $438,343 recorded for&#13;the year ended January 31, 2016 and 2015, $241,769 and $171,981 were direct costs of a stock offering and have been recorded as&#13;a reduction in additional paid in capital.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;For the years ended January 31, 2016&#13;and 2015, when computing fair value of share-based payments, the Company has considered the following variables:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td style=background-color: white; line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=background-color: white; line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=background-color: white;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right; line-height: 115%&gt;0&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;%&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right; line-height: 115%&gt;0&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;%&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The expected option term is computed&#13;using the &amp;#147;simplified&amp;#148; method as permitted under the provisions of ASC 718-10-599. The Company uses the simplified&#13;method to calculate expected term of share options and similar instruments as the Company does not have sufficient historical exercise&#13;data to provide a reasonable basis upon which to estimate expected term.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The expected stock price volatility&#13;for the Company&amp;#146;s stock options was determined by the historical volatilities for industry peers and used an average of those&#13;volatilities. Risk free interest rates were obtained from U.S. Treasury rates for the applicable periods.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Earnings (Loss) Per Share&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Basic earnings (loss) per share is computed&#13;by dividing net income (loss) by the weighted average number of shares of common stock outstanding during each period. Diluted&#13;earnings (loss) per share is computed by dividing net income (loss), adjusted for changes in income or loss that resulted from&#13;the assumed conversion of convertible shares, by the weighted average number of shares of common stock, common stock equivalents&#13;and potentially dilutive securities outstanding during the period.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times

 Times

   &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&lt;b&gt;Total common stock equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=line-height: 115%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double;  Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Since the Company reflected a net loss&#13;during the year ended January 31, 2016 and 2015, the effect of considering any common stock equivalents, would have been anti-dilutive.&#13;A separate computation of diluted earnings (loss) per share is not presented.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income Taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Income taxes are provided in accordance&#13;with ASC No. 740, &amp;#147;Accounting for Income Taxes&amp;#148;. A deferred tax asset or liability is recorded for all temporary differences&#13;between financial and tax reporting and net operating loss carryforwards. Deferred tax expense (benefit) results from the net change&#13;during the period of deferred tax assets and liabilities.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Deferred tax assets are reduced by a&#13;valuation allowance when, in the opinion of management, it is more likely than not that some portion or all of the deferred tax&#13;assets will not be realized. Deferred tax assets and liabilities are adjusted for the effects of changes in tax laws and rates&#13;on the date of enactment.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company is no longer subject to&#13;tax examinations by tax authorities for years prior to 2012.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Reclassification&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Certain prior period amounts have been&#13;reclassified to conform to current period presentation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Recent Accounting Pronouncements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In May 2014, the Financial Accounting&#13;Standards Board (&amp;#147;FASB&amp;#148;) issued Accounting Standards Update (ASU) No. 2014-09, Revenue from Contracts with Customers.&#13;The revenue recognition standard affects all entities that have contracts with customers, except for certain items. The new revenue&#13;recognition standard eliminates the transaction and industry-specific revenue recognition guidance under current GAAP and replaces&#13;it with a principle-based approach for determining revenue recognition. In July 2015, the effective date was delayed one year by&#13;a vote by the FASB. Public business entities, certain not-for-profit entities, and certain employee benefit plans would apply the&#13;guidance in ASU 2014-09 to annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017, including interim reporting periods within&#13;that reporting period. Earlier application would be permitted only as of annual reporting periods beginning after December 15,&#13;2016, including interim reporting periods within that reporting period. The Company has reviewed the applicable ASU and has not,&#13;at the current time, quantified the effects of this pronouncement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In March 2015, the Financial Accounting&#13;Standards Board issued Accounting Standards Update (ASU) No. 2015-03, Interest - Imputation of Interest (Subtopic 835-30): Simplifying&#13;the Presentation of Debt Issuance Costs. The amendments in this ASU require that debt issuance costs related to a recognized debt&#13;liability be presented in the balance sheet as a direct deduction from the carrying amount of that debt liability, consistent with&#13;debt discounts. The recognition and measurement guidance for debt issuance costs are not affected by the amendments in this ASU.&#13;The amendments are effective for financial statements issued for fiscal years beginning after December 15, 2015, and interim periods&#13;within those fiscal years. Early adoption of the amendments is permitted for financial statements that have not been previously&#13;issued. The amendments should be applied on a retrospective basis, wherein the balance sheet of each individual period presented&#13;should be adjusted to reflect the period-specific effects of applying the new guidance. Upon transition, an entity is required&#13;to comply with the applicable disclosures for a change in an accounting principle. These disclosures include the nature of and&#13;reason for the change in accounting principle, the transition method, a description of the prior-period information that has been&#13;retrospectively adjusted, and the effect of the change on the financial statement line items (i.e., debt issuance cost asset and&#13;the debt liability). The Company is currently evaluating the effects of ASU 2015-03 on the consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In July 2015, the FASB issued the FASB&#13;Accounting Standards Update No. 2015-11 &amp;#147;&lt;i&gt;Inventory (Topic 330)&lt;/i&gt;: &lt;i&gt;Simplifying the Measurement of Inventory&amp;#148;&#13;(&amp;#147;ASU 2015-11&amp;#148;). &lt;/i&gt;The amendments in this Update do not apply to inventory that is measured using last-in, first-out&#13;(LIFO) or the retail inventory method. The amendments apply to all other inventory, which includes inventory that is measured using&#13;first-in, first-out (FIFO) or average cost. An entity should measure inventory within the scope of this Update at the lower of&#13;cost and net realizable value. Net realizable value is the estimated selling prices in the ordinary course of business, less reasonably&#13;predictable costs of completion, disposal, and transportation. Subsequent measurement is unchanged for inventory measured using&#13;LIFO or the retail inventory method.&lt;i&gt; &lt;/i&gt;For public business entities, the amendments in this Update are effective for fiscal&#13;years beginning after December 15, 2016, including interim periods within those fiscal years. The Company is currently evaluating&#13;the effects of ASU 2015-11 on the consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In August 2015, the FASB issued the&#13;FASB Accounting Standards Update No. 2015-14 &amp;#147;&lt;i&gt;Revenue from Contracts with Customers (Topic 606)&lt;/i&gt;: &lt;i&gt;Deferral of the&#13;Effective Date&amp;#148; (&amp;#147;ASU 2015-14&amp;#148;). &lt;/i&gt;The amendments in this Update defer the effective date of Update 2014-09&#13;for all entities by one year. Public business entities, certain not-for-profit entities, and certain employee benefit plans should&#13;apply the guidance in Update 2014-09 to annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017, including interim reporting&#13;periods within that reporting period. Earlier application is permitted only as of annual reporting periods beginning after December&#13;15, 2016, including interim reporting periods within that reporting period. The Company is currently evaluating the effects of&#13;ASU 2015-14 on the consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.8pt&gt;In April 2015, the&#13;Financial Accounting Standards Board issued Accounting Standards Update 2015-03,&lt;i&gt; Interest-Imputation of Interest. &lt;/i&gt;To simplify&#13;presentation of debt issuance costs, the amendments in this Update would require that debt issuance costs be presented in the balance&#13;sheet as a direct deduction from the carrying amount of debt liability, consistent with debt discounts or premiums. The recognition&#13;and measurement guidance for debt issuance costs would not be affected by the amendments in this update. This Accounting Standards&#13;Update is the final version of Proposed Accounting Standards Update 2014-250-Interest-Imputation of Interest (Subtopic 835-30),&#13;which has been deleted. The amendments in this update are effective for financial statements issued for fiscal years beginning&#13;after December 15, 2015, and interim periods within those fiscal years. The adoption of ASU 2015-03 is not expected to have a material&#13;impact on our financial position, results of operations or cash flows.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In February 2016, the Financial Accounting&#13;Standards Board (&amp;#147;FASB&amp;#148;) issued Accounting Standards Update (&amp;#147;ASU&amp;#148;) No. 2016-02, &amp;#147;Leases&amp;#148; (topic&#13;842). The FASB issued this update to increase transparency and comparability among organizations by recognizing lease assets and&#13;lease liabilities on the balance sheet and disclosing key information about leasing arrangements. The updated guidance is effective&#13;for annual periods beginning after December 15, 2018, including interim periods within those fiscal years. Early adoption of the&#13;update is permitted. The Company is currently evaluating the impact of the new standard.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In March 2016, the Financial Accounting&#13;Standards Board (&amp;#147;FASB&amp;#148;) issued Accounting Standards Update (&amp;#147;ASU&amp;#148;) No. 2016-06, &amp;#147;Derivatives and&#13;Hedging&amp;#148; (topic 815). The FASB issued this update to clarify the requirements for assessing whether contingent call (put)&#13;options that can accelerate the payment of principal on debt instruments are clearly and closely related to their debt hosts. An&#13;entity performing the assessment under the amendments in this update is required to assess the embedded call (put) options solely&#13;in accordance with the four-step decision sequence. The updated guidance is effective for annual periods beginning after December&#13;15, 2016, including interim periods within those fiscal years. Early adoption of the update is permitted. The Company is currently&#13;evaluating the impact of the new standard.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In April 2016, the Financial Accounting&#13;Standards Board (&amp;#147;FASB&amp;#148;) issued Accounting Standards Update (&amp;#147;ASU&amp;#148;) No. 2016-09, &amp;#147;Compensation &amp;#150;&#13;Stock Compensation&amp;#148; (topic 718). The FASB issued this update to improve the accounting for employee share-based payments&#13;and affect all organizations that issue share-based payment awards to their employees. Several aspects of the accounting for share-based&#13;payment award transactions are simplified, including: (a) income tax consequences; (b) classification of awards as either equity&#13;or liabilities; and (c) classification on the statement of cash flows. The updated guidance is effective for annual periods beginning&#13;after December 15, 2016, including interim periods within those fiscal years. Early adoption of the update is permitted. The Company&#13;is currently evaluating the impact of the new standard.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of Estimates&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The preparation of consolidated financial&#13;statements in conformity with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles requires management to make estimates and assumptions&#13;that affect the amounts reported in the consolidated financial statements and accompanying notes. Such estimates and assumptions&#13;impact, among others, the following: allowance for doubtful accounts, inventory obsolescence and the fair value of share-based&#13;payments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company records revenue for products&#13;when all of the following have occurred: (1) persuasive evidence of an arrangement exists, (2) the product is delivered, (3) the&#13;sales price to the customer is fixed or determinable, and (4) collectability of the related customer receivable is reasonably assured.&#13;There is no stated right of return for products.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company meets these criteria upon&#13;shipment.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman
 Times
